max-w-full break-words text-start justify-self-start leading-snug">Description</div></h4><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 mx-auto page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">01.</strong> Private WebSocket connections do not require subscriptions; data is automatically pushed after a successful connection. This includes both trading messages and custom messages.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">02.</strong> Trading messages are identified with the type <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">type-event</code>. Other message types will be defined separately.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">03.</strong> The <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">event</code> field within the body of a trading message can be one of the following: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">Snapshot</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">ACCOUNT_UPDATE</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">DEPOSIT_UPDATE</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">WITHDRAW_UPDATE</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">TRANSFER_IN_UPDATE</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">TRANSFER_OUT_UPDATE</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">ORDER_UPDATE</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">FORCE_WITHDRAW_UPDATE</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">FORCE_TRADE_UPDATE</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">FUNDING_SETTLEMENT</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">ORDER_FILL_FEE_INCOME</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">START_LIQUIDATING</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">FINISH_LIQUIDATING</code>, or <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">UNRECOGNIZED</code>.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">04.</strong> Ping-Pong Mechanism:</p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;◦&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">Server Ping (Heartbeat):</strong></p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">After a successful WebSocket connection, the server sends a Ping message at a fixed interval. The message body looks like: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;ping&quot;,&quot;time&quot;:&quot;1693208170000&quot;}</code>. The <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">time</code> field is the server&#x27;s timestamp when the Ping was sent.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">The client must respond with a Pong message upon receipt, with a body like: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;pong&quot;,&quot;time&quot;:&quot;1693208170000&quot;}</code>.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">If the server doesn&#x27;t receive a Pong response after 5 consecutive Pings, the server will terminate the connection.</p></div></li></ul></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;◦&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">Client Ping (Latency Measurement):</strong></p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">After a successful WebSocket connection, the client can also initiate a Ping message with a body like: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;ping&quot;,&quot;time&quot;:&quot;1693208170000&quot;}</code>. The <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">time</code> field is the client&#x27;s timestamp when the Ping was sent.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">The server will immediately respond with a Pong message, with a body like: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;pong&quot;,&quot;time&quot;:&quot;1693208170000&quot;}</code>. The <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">time</code> field in the Pong will match the <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">time</code> field in the client&#x27;s Ping.</p></div></li></ul></div></li></ul></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">05.</strong> Authentication:</p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;◦&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">Web:</strong></p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">Browsers don&#x27;t allow custom headers during WebSocket connections, so special handling is required.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">Use the same authentication logic as HTTP. Create a JSON string using the <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">X-edgeX-Api-Signature</code>, <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">X-edgeX-Api-Timestamp</code> key-value pairs, for example: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;X-edgeX-Api-Signature&quot;: &quot;00e6b34cf9c3c0ca407cc2fe149fad836206c97201f236137c0e89fd079760470672b5257fa372710b5863d1ec6e0215e5bd6b2c3a319eda88886250a100524706ea3dd81a7fc864893c8c6f674e4a4510c369f939bdc0259a0980dfde882c2d&quot;, &quot;X-edgeX-Api-Timestamp&quot;: &quot;1705720068228&quot;}</code>.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">Base64 encode this JSON string.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">During the WebSocket request, pass the base64 encoded value in the <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">SEC_WEBSOCKET_PROTOCOL</code> header.</p></div></li></ul></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;◦&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">App/API:</strong></p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">App/API WebSocket connections can use <a class="underline decoration-[max(0.07em,1px)] underline-offset-2 links-accent:underline-offset-4 links-default:decoration-primary/6 links-default:text-primary-subtle hover:links-default:text-primary-strong contrast-more:links-default:text-primary contrast-more:hover:links-default:text-primary-strong links-accent:decoration-primary-subtle hover:links-accent:decoration-[3px] hover:links-accent:[text-decoration-skip-ink:none] transition-all duration-100" href="/edgeX-documentation/api/authentication#private-api">custom</a> headers. Therefore, Apps/API can continue using the same authentication logic as HTTP, or they can use the Web authentication method described above.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">WebSocket is a GET request and there is no need to sign the request body.</p></div></li></ul></div></li></ul></div></li></ul><h4 id="url-api-v1-private-ws" class="text-xl font-semibold heading flex items-baseline class="relative hash grid grid-area-1-1 h-[1em] border-0 opacity-0 group-hover/hash:opacity-[0] group-focus/hash:opacity-[0] md:group-hover/hash:opacity-[1] md:group-focus/hash:opacity-[1] -ml-6 pr-2"><a href="#description-1" aria-label="Direct link to heading" class="inline-flex h-full items-start leading-snug"><svg style="mask-image:url(https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v6.6.0/svgs/regular/hashtag.svg?v=2&amp;token=a463935e93);-webkit-mask-image:url(https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v6.6.0/svgs/regular/hashtag.svg?v=2&amp;token=a463935e93);mask-repeat:no-repeat;-webkit-mask-repeat:no-repeat;mask-position:center;-webkit-mask-position:center" max-w-full break-words text-start justify-self-start leading-snug">Description</div></h4><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 mx-auto page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">01.</strong> When subscribing or unsubscribing, the server will validate the channel. For invalid channels, the server will respond with an error message, for example: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;error&quot;,&quot;content&quot;:{&quot;code&quot;:&quot;INVALID_CONTRACT_ID&quot;&quot;msg&quot;:&quot;invalid contractId:100000001&quot;}}</code></p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">02.</strong> The message structure for subscribing and unsubscribing is: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;: &quot;subscribe&quot;, &quot;channel&quot;: &quot;ticker.10000001&quot;}</code>.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;•&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">03.</strong> Ping-Pong Mechanism:</p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;◦&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">Server Ping (Heartbeat):</strong></p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">After a successful WebSocket connection, the server sends a Ping message at a fixed interval. The message body looks like: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;ping&quot;,&quot;time&quot;:&quot;1693208170000&quot;}</code>. The <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">time</code> field is the server&#x27;s timestamp when the Ping was sent.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">The client must respond with a Pong message upon receipt, with a body like: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;pong&quot;,&quot;time&quot;:&quot;1693208170000&quot;}</code>.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">If the server doesn&#x27;t receive a Pong response after 5 consecutive Pings, the server will terminate the connection.</p></div></li></ul></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start"><strong class="font-bold">Client Ping (Latency Measurement):</strong></p><ul class="min-w-0 space-y-2 page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0"><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">After a successful WebSocket connection, the client can also initiate a Ping message with a body like: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;ping&quot;,&quot;time&quot;:&quot;1693208170000&quot;}</code>. The <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">time</code> field is the client&#x27;s timestamp when the Ping was sent.</p></div></li><li class="leading-normal flex items-start"><div class="text-base leading-normal mr-1 flex min-h-lh min-w-6 items-center justify-center text-tint"><div class="before:font-var before:content-(--pseudoBefore--content)" style="--pseudoBefore--content:&#x27;▪&#x27;;--font-family:Arial;font-size:min(1.5em, 24px);line-height:1"></div></div><div class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col space-y-2"><p class="page-width-wide:mx-0 w-full decoration-primary/6 print:break-inside-avoid max-w-3xl min-h-lh flip-heading-hash [h2]:pt-0 [h3]:pt-0 [h4]:pt-0 mx-0 text-start justify-self-start">The server will immediately respond with a Pong message, with a body like: <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;pong&quot;,&quot;time&quot;:&quot;1693208170000&quot;}</code>. The <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">time</code> field in the Pong will match the <code class="py-px px-1.5 min-w-6.5 justify-center items-center ring-1 ring-inset ring-tint bg-tint rounded-sm text-[.875em] leading-[calc(max(1.20em,1.25rem))]">time</code> field in the client&#x27;s Ping.</p></div></li></ul></div></li></ul></div></li></ul><h4 id="subscription-metadata" class="text-xl font-semibold heading flex items-baseline scroll-mt-(--content-scroll-margin)
